; Technical specification of configuration options
;
; tinyTwofish is highly configurable in its Flash/SRAM footprint; by altering options in
; 2fish_avr.cfg a desirable trade-off between footprint and efficiency can be selected.
;
; The list below shows all potentially useful combinations; sorted in order by:
;
; 1) KEY_SIZE
; 2) SRAM requirements
; 3) Program size
;
; All measurements were taken for the case STATIC=0
;
; SIZE  Actual footprint of code + tables (excl. alignment)
; ASIZE Minimum amount of flash necessary to load (incl. alignment)
; SRAM  Total amount of SRAM needed (.bss and stack)
; INIT	Cycles needed for one-time initialization
; KS    Cycles needed for keyscheduling
; EB    Cycles needed to encrypt one block
; KE    Cycles needed to keyschedule & encrypt one block
